Each percentages of these five categories in the particulate matter were calculated, and the results were shown in Fig. 7. The proportions of OC, EC, water-soluble ions and inorganic elements in gasoline vehicles were  $53.93\\%$ $13.07\\%$ $13.12\\%$  and  $0.30\\%$  respectively.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Comparison of measured and model-calculated real-w', 'text': 'The basic objective of BAB II was the evaluation of an emission model under real-world conditions, including the evaluation of emission factors and statistical traffic data used in the model. Therefore, a concept of measurements up- and downwind of a motorway was developed and tested in 1997 (Vogel et al., 2000) and implemented in 2001. The mass balancing method chosen requires accurate measurements upwind and downwind of the motorway. Hence, a rigorous quality assurance programme has to be applied before and after the field phase. Furthermore, it is essential to monitor the traffic on the motorway for the determination of source strengths from measurements and for model\n\ncalculations with given emission factors. During the BAB II field phase, a detailed traffic census was carried out, providing information of the number of vehicles passing by on the motorway, the speed of the vehicles, the composition of the car fleet, and the engine and exhaust gas reduction techniques. A period of two days when the motorway was closed due to construction work was used to demonstrate that with wind perpendicular to the motorway, plumes downwind of the motorway clearly originate from the traffic passing by Kohler et al., (2005).\n\nSummarising, there are disadvantages of the method chosen, e.g. (i) dependency on meteorological conditions, (ii) experimental complexity and sensitivity due to difference calculations, and (iii) errors caused by few unidentified vehicles with extreme emissions ("high emitters").                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Comparison of measured and model-calculated real-w', 'text': 'This concept is based on the measurement of concentrations on the windward and the lee side of a motorway and on the assumption of homogeneous conditions for all parameters along the respective road section (Vogel et al., 2000; Corsmeier et al., 2005). In this case, source strengths of gaseous and particulate vehicle emissions can be determined by measuring the vertical profiles of the concentrations of the substances and the horizontal wind speed over the height of the plume of the specific compound on the lee side of the motorway, as well as by the respective windward profiles.\n\nThe BAB II concept includes symmetric, continuous profile measurements of NO,  $\\mathrm{NO}_x$ , CO,  $\\mathrm{O}_3$ , and\n\nnumerous NMHC compounds as well as of PM on both sides of the motorway and measurements of meteorological parameters. A detailed traffic census, taking into account the different layers of vehicles, was carried out. Using an emission calculation model, statistical traffic data, and traffic census results, the calculated emissions are finally evaluated against the emissions measured. Additionally, the traffic census was used to check whether the predictions made by the Umweltbundesamt, UBA (German Environmental Protection Agency) in 1997 with respect to the degree of exhaust gas reduction technologies used in the vehicle fleet had come true (UBA, 1997).\n\nAs this paper summarises the BAB II results and compares measured and model calculated emissions, for detailed information about the determination of source strengths, traffic census data and model development look up the specific contributions within this special issue. For the overall project description see Corsmeier et al. (2005). The source strengths for CO and  $\\mathrm{NO}_x$  are given by Kohler et al. (2005), those for NMHC compounds by Petrea et al. (2005). PM emissions are investigated by Rosenbohm et al. (2005) and Imhof et al.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Biomass burning emissions estimated with a global ', 'text': 'The FRP to dry matter combusted conversion factors derived by Heil et al. (2012) result in a distribution and magnitude of the C combustion rate of GFASv1.0 that is consistent with the GFED3.1 inventory within its accuracy. However, distinct differences exist, most notably more widespread biomass burning with low combustion rates. Some of the additional signal is spuriously caused by remaining gas flares, industrial activity and, possibly, occasional MODIS FRP values of doubtful quality. Nevertheless, the main effect is attributed to a lower detection threshold of the FRP-based approach than the approach based on burnt area.\n\nSimulations of atmospheric aerosols using the global MACC system with and without MODIS AOD assimilation show that a model based on the GFASv1.0 emissions of OC and BC can be made consistent with the analysis, and consequently the MODIS AOD observations, when the AOD due to the OM and BC fields is enhanced by a factor of 3.4. Since all aerosol sink processes are linear, the average AOD of an aerosol species scales linearly with its source strength. Therefore, we recommend to correct the OM and BC emission estimates of GFASv1.0 with a factor of 3.4 when using them in the global MACC aerosol forecasting system. The recommendation would equally apply to GFED3.1 since its budgets are consistent with GFASv1.0.\n\nThe recommended enhancement of the aerosol emissions in the MACC systems is consistent with findings in recent major top-down emission estimates but inconsistent with bottom-up estimates. Under the assumption that the MODIS AOD observations are sufficiently accurate, the inconsistency between the two approaches can originate from errors in the biomass combustion estimates, inaccuracies in the emissions factors, an inadequate representation of aerosols and their source and sink processes in the models, or erroneous optical properties of smoke in the models.', 'summary': 'The FRP to dry matter combusted conversion factors derived by Heil et al. In high-concentration-gradient regions, such as street canyons and roadway tunnels, VIT can significantly influence exhaust pollutant accumulation patterns (Shi et al., 2019). Laminar (i.e., streamline) flow is dominant in railway tunnels because the train fills most of the tunnel area and travels at relatively high speeds. In roadway tunnels, turbulent flow seldom occurs because of the large unoccupied area and relatively slow movement of vehicles (Niu et al., 2020). In this study, the gridded open fire emissions from the FINN are vertically distributed in the PBL  $(65\\%)$  and upper atmosphere  $(35\\%)$ .\n\n# 2.4. Inverse modeling of  $NO_{x}$  and NMVOCs emissions\n\nGiven the relatively short lifetime of  $\\mathrm{NO}_2$  and HCHO, their satellite columns often correlate with  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{x}}$  and NMVOCs emissions and can be applied to estimations of top-down emission inventories. We proceed the inverse modeling for total  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{x}}$  and NMVOCs emissions after combining anthropogenic, biogenic, and biomass burning emissions. To constrain bottom-up emissions of total  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{x}}$  and NMVOCs, we apply the Gauss-Newton method, an analytical inversion approach to finding solutions to problems that are not rigorously nonlinear, described in Rodgers (2000). This approach assumes no correlation between observations and emission errors, and the error covariances of observations and emissions with zero bias Gaussian probability density functions. The inversions with the Newtonian iterations gradually approach convergence at the zero of the gradients of the cost function, shown in Eq. (1). Posteriori emissions can be estimated by Eq. (2).\n\n$$\nJ (x) = \\frac {1}{2} (y - F (x)) ^ {T} S _ {o} ^ {- 1} (y - F (x)) + \\frac {1}{2} (x - x _ {a}) ^ {T} S _ {e} ^ {- 1} (x - x _ {a}) \\tag {1}\n$$\n\n$$\nx _ {i + 1} = x _ {a} + S _ {e} K _ {i} ^ {T} \\left(K _ {i} S _ {e} K _ {i} ^ {T} + S _ {o}\\right) ^ {- 1} \\left[ y - F \\left(x _ {i}\\right) + K _ {i} \\left(x _ {i} - x _ {a}\\right) \\right] \\tag {2}\n$$\n\nwhere  $x$  and  $x_{a}$  represent a posteriori and a priori emissions,', 'summary': 'For biomass burning emissions, we refer to the Fire Inventory from National Center for Atmospheric Research (FINN) version 1.5, which provides daily g...'}, 来自论文ID: changes_in_the_ozone_chemical_regime_over_the_cont_1, 关键词: None

The improved emission inventory substantially enhances the capability of the regional air quality model in reproducing the  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  concentrations particularly during biomass burning events. Given the important role of aerosol direct radiative effects in modulating the meteorological conditions as well as the subsequent governance on aerosol concentrations, numerical sensitivity experiments reveal that\n\nthe aerosols emitted by biomass burning strikingly steer the development of the PBL by changing meteorological conditions, which then subsequently induce the accumulation of  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  concentrations.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Mobile measurement of vehicle emission factors in ', 'text': 'The average  $\\mathrm{PM}_{10}$  and  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  concentrations were in the ranges of 41.0-87.5 and  $23.5 - 41.3\\mu \\mathrm{g}\\mathrm{m}^{-3}$ , respectively. The PM concentrations varied substantially compared with the other pollutants (Fig. 2g and h). The maximum  $\\mathrm{PM}_{10}$  concentration  $(188\\mu \\mathrm{g}\\mathrm{m}^{-3})$  was observed when the mobile laboratory passed next to a HDDV, indicating that PM can be strongly affected by the number of HDDVs on the road, which accounted for a relatively high proportion  $(9\\%)$  of the traffic volume in the SJT. Non-combustion PM sources in the road environment include tire wear, brake abrasion, and resuspended dust (Abu-Allaban et al., 2003). Because photochemical reactions are rare in tunnels, the main contributors of  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  were primary sources, i.e., elemental carbon and primary organic aerosols from vehicle emissions and small particles from non-combustion emissions. The  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5} / \\mathrm{PM}_{10}$  ratio remained relatively constant during the campaign (approximately 0.5), indicative of the mixed effects of vehicle combustion and non-combustion sources. Based on an improved emission inventory of the Visible Infrared Imaging Radiometer Suite (VIIRS) relative to commonly used Global Fire Emissions Database (GFED), we thoroughly evaluate the impact of biomass burning on air quality and climate during the episodes of November 2017 in Northeast China which is rich in agriculture burning.                         具体而言评估人员总结条目内容为冬季需严格VOCs控制以缓解PM2.5污染，但当前OFP/SOAP评估方法存在局限：排放清单法依赖外部排放因子误差大，实地测量法因缺乏多源同步数据难以确定关键贡献源。,理由是精准指出PM2.5控制痛点（方法学缺陷）并给出具体案例（汽油蒸发/溶剂使用等来源评估），为优化评估体系提供突破方向。,他抽取处理一些关键词推荐给你['speciated emission inventory', 'SOAP quantification', 'source-resolved OFP']。
                        这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Source apportionment of volatile organic compounds', 'text': 'Currently, stringent controls on VOCs are needed to mitigate  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  pollution in winter (Huang et al., 2014). The estimation of ozone formation potential (OFP) and SOA of each VOC source is vital before cost-effective strategies can be carried out. Indeed, many researches have been done on determining the most reactive VOC sources. Generally, there are two methods to estimate the OFP or SOA formation potential (SOAP) of each VOC source. One is the speciated VOC emission inventory (Zheng et al., 2009; Liang et al., 2017; Wu et al., 2017; Wu and Xie, 2017) and the other refers to the field measurement of VOC profiles from source emissions. The emission inventory method is sensitive to emission factors, and most of these speciated inventory studies in China always adopted emission factors from studies conducted in foreign countries or other regions, which had large uncertainty (Zhang et al., 2013; Wang, 2014; Wu and Xie, 2017). The local VOC emission inventory is still insufficient (Li et al., 2017), mainly due to the complexity of obtaining emission factors and accurate source activity data.\n\nMeanwhile, the source-specific measurements and emission inventory establishing works are costly. In practice, the estimation of photochemical characteristics (i.e., OFP) with measured VOC source profiles is continuously being reported.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Long-term observations of oxygenated volatile orga', 'text': 'Oxygenated volatile organic compounds (OVOCs) are important precursors and intermediate products of atmospheric photochemical reactions, which can promote the formation of secondary pollutants such as ozone  $(\\mathrm{O}_3)$  and secondary organic aerosol (SOA). However, there have been few studies on the sources of and long-term variation in ambient OVOCs. This study combined sensitive, near real-time measurements of VOCs by proton transfer reaction-mass spectrometry (PTR-MS) with an improved photochemical age parameterization method to quantify daytime sources of OVOCs in an urban atmosphere in China from 2014 to 2019, permitting the observation of the impacts of emission control strategies that were implemented during this period. Temporal variation in six key OVOCs (methanol, acetaldehyde, acetone, methyl ethyl ketone (MEK), formic acid, and acetic acid) were observed. The sum of concentrations of OVOCs was averagely  $13\\%$  higher during the dry season (November to April), when winds transported polluted air masses to Shenzhen from the continent, than during the wet season, and peak diurnal levels occurred during the daytime year-round due to photochemical production and higher daytime anthropogenic emissions. The average dry season concentration of OVOCs declined from a peak of 30.3 ppb in 2015 to 18.7 ppb in 2019. The results of source apportionment showed that primary anthropogenic sources contributed the most to methanol, MEK, and acetic acid  $(32 - 51\\%)$ ; the dominant sources of acetaldehyde and formic acid were both primary and secondary anthropogenic sources; and biomass burning contributed a small fraction  $(5 - 11\\%)$  to the six OVOCs. From 2014 to 2019, contributions from primary anthropogenic sources of OVOCs decreased significantly by  $50 - 60\\%$  due to intensive pollution control measures in Shenzhen, whereas pollution control measures had no observable impact on secondary OVOCs, indicating their formation was not limited by availability of their primary VOC precursors.', 'summary': 'Oxygenated volatile organic compounds (OVOCs) are important precursors and intermediate products of atmospheric photochemical reactions, which can pro...'}, 来自论文ID: long-term_observations_of_oxygenated_volatile_orga, 关键词: None

                        这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Changes in the ozone chemical regime over the cont', 'text': 'For biomass burning emissions, we refer to the Fire Inventory from National Center for Atmospheric Research (FINN) version 1.5, which provides daily global estimates of trace gas and particulate matter emissions based on observation by the Moderate Resolution Imaging Spectroradiometer (MODIS) (Wiedinmyer et al., 2014, 2011, 2006). In this study, the gridded open fire emissions from the FINN are vertically distributed in the PBL  $(65\\%)$  and upper atmosphere  $(35\\%)$ .\n\n# 2.4. Inverse modeling of  $NO_{x}$  and NMVOCs emissions\n\nGiven the relatively short lifetime of  $\\mathrm{NO}_2$  and HCHO, their satellite columns often correlate with  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{x}}$  and NMVOCs emissions and can be applied to estimations of top-down emission inventories. We proceed the inverse modeling for total  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{x}}$  and NMVOCs emissions after combining anthropogenic, biogenic, and biomass burning emissions. To constrain bottom-up emissions of total  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{x}}$  and NMVOCs, we apply the Gauss-Newton method, an analytical inversion approach to finding solutions to problems that are not rigorously nonlinear, described in Rodgers (2000). This approach assumes no correlation between observations and emission errors, and the error covariances of observations and emissions with zero bias Gaussian probability density functions. The inversions with the Newtonian iterations gradually approach convergence at the zero of the gradients of the cost function, shown in Eq. (1). Posteriori emissions can be estimated by Eq. (2).\n\n$$\nJ (x) = \\frac {1}{2} (y - F (x)) ^ {T} S _ {o} ^ {- 1} (y - F (x)) + \\frac {1}{2} (x - x _ {a}) ^ {T} S _ {e} ^ {- 1} (x - x _ {a}) \\tag {1}\n$$\n\n$$\nx _ {i + 1} = x _ {a} + S _ {e} K _ {i} ^ {T} \\left(K _ {i} S _ {e} K _ {i} ^ {T} + S _ {o}\\right) ^ {- 1} \\left[ y - F \\left(x _ {i}\\right) + K _ {i} \\left(x _ {i} - x _ {a}\\right) \\right] \\tag {2}\n$$\n\nwhere  $x$  and  $x_{a}$  represent a posteriori and a priori emissions,', 'summary': 'For biomass burning emissions, we refer to the Fire Inventory from National Center for Atmospheric Research (FINN) version 1.5, which provides daily g...'}, 来自论文ID: changes_in_the_ozone_chemical_regime_over_the_cont, 关键词: None

BVOCs are important precursors of ozone and secondary organic aerosols (SOAs) (Kavouras et al., 1998; Claeys et al., 2004); therefore, it is important to understand the variability of BVOC emission and its impact on air quality and the climate system. The emission of BVOC is controlled by multiple environmental factors like temperature, radiation,  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$  concentration and other stresses. Therefore it is affected by climate changes (Guenther et al., 1995; Arneth et al., 2007; Penuelas and Staudt, 2010). Besides the climatic factors, land cover change also plays a key role in the variability of BVOC emission (Stavrakou et al., 2014; Unger, 2013; Chen et al., 2018). The proportions of OC, EC, water-soluble ions and inorganic elements in diesel vehicles were  $51.15\\%$ $25.17\\%$ $14.53\\%$  and  $0.44\\%$  respectively. Thus, the largest difference in the proportion of various components in  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  emitted from gasoline and diesel vehicles was EC.\n\n# 4.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Extension of an assessment model of ship traffic e', 'text': 'Information is currently scarce especially regarding the geographical distribution and chemical composition of PM emissions arising from ship traffic, and the chemical composition details have not commonly been introduced to global inventories of ship emissions. Corbett et al. (2010) subdivided PM from marine traffic into organic carbon and black carbon. They did not allow for the dependency on engine load of the constituents of PM; instead, fixed, predetermined loads were used for main and auxiliary engines. However, the emissions of both the various chemical components of PM and CO are sensitive to engine load. The classifications of PM components, and the detailed definitions of such classes also can vary, depending on the measurement techniques used. For instance, the experimental methods using absorptive techniques often provide black carbon (Eyring et al., 2010), but chemical techniques report a division to elemental and organic carbon. Clearly, black carbon and elemental carbon cannot be used as synonymous expressions, since there are components of organic carbon, which also absorb light (e.g. Andreae and Gelencsér, 2006).', 'summary': 'Information is currently scarce especially regarding the geographical distribution and chemical composition of PM emissions arising from ship traffic,...'}, 来自论文ID: extension_of_an_assessment_model_of_ship_traffic_e, 关键词: None

                        这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'On-road emissions of fine particles and associated', 'text': 'Vehicle emission is an important contributor to urban air pollution with the increasing number of motor vehicles. Ten typical vehicles were selected in Wuhan to study the emissions of fine particular matters  $\\mathrm{(PM_{2.5})}$  and associated chemical components by on-road tests through a Portable Emission Monitoring System (PEMS). The emission factors of  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  and the compositions of it from different types of vehicle were obtained. Results showed that the average emission factors of  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  from gasoline and diesel vehicles were 1.266 and  $16.589\\mathrm{mg}/$  km. As the emission standard of vehicles increased from China III to China V,  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  emission factor gradually decreased from 17.385 to  $1.520~\\mathrm{mg / km}$ . Emission rate of  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  was  $0.0384~\\mathrm{mg / s}$  under low speed, and it increased to 0.0775 and  $0.0964~\\mathrm{mg / s}$  under the medium and high speeds. The ratio of organic carbon versus elemental carbon (OC/EC) in  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  from gasoline vehicles was 6.89, which was greater than that of diesel vehicles as 3.12. Because gasoline was made of small molecules and the compression ratio of gasoline engine was relatively low, some OC remained in the area where the ignition failed in the cylinder. The top four water-soluble ions with high emission factors were  $\\mathrm{Cl}^-$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_4^{2 - }$ ,  $\\mathrm{Ca}^{2 + }$ , and  $\\mathrm{Na}^{+}$ , while K, Na, Ca and Mg had a larger emission factors in the 21 tested inorganic elements. These water-soluble ions and inorganic elements mainly came from the oil burning, fuel additives and engines wear. Results of  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  emission characteristics would help to improve the air quality in Wuhan.\n\n# 1. These methods mainly include remote sensing detection, vehicle bench test, tunnel test and portable vehicle emission measurement (Giechaskiel et al., 2018; Mahesh et al., 2018; Yang et al., 2020a, b). Remote sensing is an effective and economic tool to monitor vehicle emissions, while it is accurate in identifying gasoline vehicles but not diesel ones (Huang et al., 2018). And the chemical composition of  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  can not be obtained by remote sensing (Smit et al., 2019). Myung et al. (2009) carried out bench tests on light motor vehicles and found that  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  emissions of using liquefied petroleum gas and biodiesel were much lower than those of gasoline and diesel. Carbonaceous components in  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  emitted from vehicles could be studied through a bench test, and it found that the driving speed directly affected the EC emissions (Fraser et al., 2002). However, the fluence of actual driving conditions on vehicle emissions could not be reflected (Pouresmaeili et al., 2018). Sánchez et al. (2019) studied the  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  emission factors of both light and heavy vehicles through tunnel experiments, and the emission factors of heavy vehicles tended to be much higher than those of light vehicles. Since tunnels in different locations have different speed limits, and it is difficult to cover both high-speed and real-world driving conditions in some tunnels (Huang et al., 2017; Smit et al., 2017; Yang et al., 2020a, b). Because photochemical reactions are rare in tunnels, the main contributors of  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  were primary sources, i.e., elemental carbon and primary organic aerosols from vehicle emissions and small particles from non-combustion emissions. To investigate how vehicle emissions vary under the different working conditions, emission factors of CO, HC, and  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{x}}$  were divided into 11 groups according to driving speeds.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'An improved representation of fire non-methane org', 'text': 'Various terms have been used in the literature to describe reactive carbon-containing trace gases, including one of the first, non-methane hydrocarbons (NMHCs), which excludes species with oxygen or other heteroatoms. The term volatile organic compound (VOC) encompasses this broader set of compounds, although there is no agreed upon, quantitative definition for VOCs or their surrogate, non-methane organic compounds (NMOCs). The European Union defines VOC as any organic compound having an initial boiling point less than or equal to  $250^{\\circ}\\mathrm{C}$  measured at a standard atmospheric pressure of  $101.3\\mathrm{kPa}$  (European Union, 1999). The US EPA\n\ndefines VOCs as any compound that participates in atmospheric photochemical reactions except for those that they designate as having minimal reactivity. The term oxygenated VOC (OVOC) (Goldstein and Galbally, 2007; Kwan et al., 2006) has further blurred these definitions, with colloquial usage sometimes being ambiguous as to whether OVOCs are a subset of VOCs or whether VOCs represent the un-oxygenated (i.e., non-methane hydrocarbon, NMHC) suite of compounds. Volatility-based nomenclature separates VOCs from semi-volatile OC (SVOC) and intermediate-volatility OC (IVOC) species (Robinson et al., 2007). For this study, we use NMOGs, which encompasses all gas-phase organic compounds (excluding methane), regardless of volatility, degree of oxygenation, or other chemical properties.', 'summary': 'Various terms have been used in the literature to describe reactive carbon-containing trace gases, including one of the first, non-methane hydrocarbon...'}, 来自论文ID: an_improved_representation_of_fire_non-methane_org, 关键词: None

                        这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Comparison of measured and model-calculated real-w', 'text': '# 1.3. Shortcomings of emission models\n\nEmission calculation models are frequently used to determine input data for numerical modelling of summer smog events or climate change scenarios. Model-calculated emission estimates are necessary for environmental risk assessments and for settling many questions related to public health. Although significant progress was achieved in emission modelling during the last decade, there are still some serious shortcomings of the emission models, which constrict the usage of the models or limit the results of the emission calculations. This means that quantitative information about the quality of model-calculated emissions based on general traffic databases and roller test stand investigations of selected types of motors is rather poor. Especially the transferability of emission factors investigated in the laboratory to real-world traffic conditions seems to be problematic in many cases. The same applies to the model assumptions regarding the composition of the vehicle fleet, the driving pattern of individual cars, and the daily and weekly cycles of traffic load on different types of roads. Information about gaseous emissions is lacking and knowledge of particulate emissions is even poorer. Size distributions and masses of particulate matter (PM) emitted by vehicles are unknown both near the source as well as further downstream. Several attempts using different concepts have been made in the past to overcome the shortcomings mentioned. Within BAB II, a mass balance concept under real-world traffic and atmospheric conditions was investigated to evaluate the results of an emission model. Evaluated emission models are useful tools for sophisticated emission calculations and forecasts. Utilizing such tools, the efficiency of future emission reduction strategies can be determined, consequences of new traffic routes for the residents can be calculated, and reliable ozone predictions can be made, among other applications.\n\n# 1.4. The BAB II concept', 'summary': '# 1.3. Shortcomings of emission models\n\nEmission calculation models are frequently used to determine input data for numerical modelling of summer smog...'}, 来自论文ID: comparison_of_measured_and_model-calculated_real-w, 关键词: None

Therefore, a concept of measurements up- and downwind of a motorway was developed and tested in 1997 (Vogel et al., 2000) and implemented in 2001. A period of two days when the motorway was closed due to construction work was used to demonstrate that with wind perpendicular to the motorway, plumes downwind of the motorway clearly originate from the traffic passing by Kohler et al., (2005).\n\nSummarising, there are disadvantages of the method chosen, e.g. (i) dependency on meteorological conditions, (ii) experimental complexity and sensitivity due to difference calculations, and (iii) errors caused by few unidentified vehicles with extreme emissions ("high emitters"). Corbett et al. (2010) subdivided PM from marine traffic into organic carbon and black carbon. They did not allow for the dependency on engine load of the constituents of PM; instead, fixed, predetermined loads were used for main and auxiliary engines. However, the emissions of both the various chemical components of PM and CO are sensitive to engine load. The classifications of PM components, and the detailed definitions of such classes also can vary, depending on the measurement techniques used. For instance, the experimental methods using absorptive techniques often provide black carbon (Eyring et al., 2010), but chemical techniques report a division to elemental and organic carbon. If the importance of atmospheric photochemical processes exceeds the differences of emission profiles from various sources, the factors in PMF can still be identified according to the different degrees of photochemical processing (Yuan et al., 2012).                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Long-term observations of oxygenated volatile orga', 'text': '© 2020 Elsevier Ltd. All rights reserved.\n\n# Credit author contribution statement\n\nShi-Yong Xia: Methodology, Writing - original draft. Chuan Wang: Data curation, Formal analysis. Bo Zhu: Conceptualization, Data curation. Xue Chen: Data curation. Ning Feng: Formal analysis. Guang-He Yu: Conceptualization, Supervision. Xiao-Feng Huang: Methodology, Conceptualization, Writing - review & editing.\n\n# 1. Introduction\n\nVolatile organic compounds (VOCs) are important precursors that can undergo atmospheric photochemical reactions with nitrogen oxides  $\\left(\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{x}}\\right)$  under ultraviolet radiation to produce secondary products such as ozone  $\\left(\\mathrm{O}_{3}\\right)$  and peroxyacetyl nitrate (PAN) and form photochemical smog (Derwent et al., 2003; Seinfeld and Pandis, 2016). Oxygenated volatile organic compounds (OVOCs) are a class of VOCs with oxygen-containing functional groups, mainly composed of aldehydes, ketones, and alcohols. The concentrations of atmospheric OVOCs vary greatly in different regions. Studies in clean marine areas showed that although phytoplankton in the marine may release OVOCs, such as methanol, acetaldehyde and acetone, their ambient air mixing ratios were usually only a few\n\nto a few hundred pptv (Galbally et al., 2007; Colomb et al., 2009; Wohl et al., 2020), while the concentrations of OVOCs in polluted areas can be as high as dozens of ppbv (Seinfeld and Pandis, 2016; Sheng et al., 2018; Zhou et al., 2019; Maji et al., 2020). The variation in OVOC concentrations is due to the wide variety and complexity of sources of OVOCs. OVOCs can be directly emitted by anthropogenic sources, e.g., solvent volatilization, vehicle emissions (Legreid et al., 2007; Ou et al., 2015), and biogenic sources (Jacob et al., 2002; Mellouki et al., 2015). In addition, OVOCs can also be formed as secondary products by photochemical oxidation of nonmethane hydrocarbons (NMHCs) from anthropogenic and biogenic sources (Yuan et al., 2012; Liu et al., 2015).', 'summary': '© 2020 Elsevier Ltd. All rights reserved.\n\n# Credit author contribution statement\n\nShi-Yong Xia: Methodology, Writing - original draft. Chuan Wang: Da...'}, 来自论文ID: long-term_observations_of_oxygenated_volatile_orga, 关键词: None

                        这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Comparison of measured and model-calculated real-w', 'text': 'This concept is based on the measurement of concentrations on the windward and the lee side of a motorway and on the assumption of homogeneous conditions for all parameters along the respective road section (Vogel et al., 2000; Corsmeier et al., 2005). In this case, source strengths of gaseous and particulate vehicle emissions can be determined by measuring the vertical profiles of the concentrations of the substances and the horizontal wind speed over the height of the plume of the specific compound on the lee side of the motorway, as well as by the respective windward profiles.\n\nThe BAB II concept includes symmetric, continuous profile measurements of NO,  $\\mathrm{NO}_x$ , CO,  $\\mathrm{O}_3$ , and\n\nnumerous NMHC compounds as well as of PM on both sides of the motorway and measurements of meteorological parameters. A detailed traffic census, taking into account the different layers of vehicles, was carried out. Using an emission calculation model, statistical traffic data, and traffic census results, the calculated emissions are finally evaluated against the emissions measured. Additionally, the traffic census was used to check whether the predictions made by the Umweltbundesamt, UBA (German Environmental Protection Agency) in 1997 with respect to the degree of exhaust gas reduction technologies used in the vehicle fleet had come true (UBA, 1997).\n\nAs this paper summarises the BAB II results and compares measured and model calculated emissions, for detailed information about the determination of source strengths, traffic census data and model development look up the specific contributions within this special issue. For the overall project description see Corsmeier et al. (2005). The source strengths for CO and  $\\mathrm{NO}_x$  are given by Kohler et al. (2005), those for NMHC compounds by Petrea et al. (2005). PM emissions are investigated by Rosenbohm et al. (2005) and Imhof et al. (2005) and finally the emission model calculations and the traffic measurements are presented by Kuhlwein and Friedrich (2005).', 'summary': 'This concept is based on the measurement of concentrations on the windward and the lee side of a motorway and on the assumption of homogeneous conditi...'}, 来自论文ID: comparison_of_measured_and_model-calculated_real-w, 关键词: None

Introduction\n\n# 1.1.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Biomass burning emissions estimated with a global ', 'text': 'The FRP to dry matter combusted conversion factors derived by Heil et al. (2012) result in a distribution and magnitude of the C combustion rate of GFASv1.0 that is consistent with the GFED3.1 inventory within its accuracy. However, distinct differences exist, most notably more widespread biomass burning with low combustion rates. Some of the additional signal is spuriously caused by remaining gas flares, industrial activity and, possibly, occasional MODIS FRP values of doubtful quality. Nevertheless, the main effect is attributed to a lower detection threshold of the FRP-based approach than the approach based on burnt area.\n\nSimulations of atmospheric aerosols using the global MACC system with and without MODIS AOD assimilation show that a model based on the GFASv1.0 emissions of OC and BC can be made consistent with the analysis, and consequently the MODIS AOD observations, when the AOD due to the OM and BC fields is enhanced by a factor of 3.4. Since all aerosol sink processes are linear, the average AOD of an aerosol species scales linearly with its source strength. Therefore, we recommend to correct the OM and BC emission estimates of GFASv1.0 with a factor of 3.4 when using them in the global MACC aerosol forecasting system. The recommendation would equally apply to GFED3.1 since its budgets are consistent with GFASv1.0.\n\nThe recommended enhancement of the aerosol emissions in the MACC systems is consistent with findings in recent major top-down emission estimates but inconsistent with bottom-up estimates. Under the assumption that the MODIS AOD observations are sufficiently accurate, the inconsistency between the two approaches can originate from errors in the biomass combustion estimates, inaccuracies in the emissions factors, an inadequate representation of aerosols and their source and sink processes in the models, or erroneous optical properties of smoke in the models.', 'summary': 'The FRP to dry matter combusted conversion factors derived by Heil et al.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Comparison of measured and model-calculated real-w', 'text': '# 1.3. Shortcomings of emission models\n\nEmission calculation models are frequently used to determine input data for numerical modelling of summer smog events or climate change scenarios. Model-calculated emission estimates are necessary for environmental risk assessments and for settling many questions related to public health. Although significant progress was achieved in emission modelling during the last decade, there are still some serious shortcomings of the emission models, which constrict the usage of the models or limit the results of the emission calculations. This means that quantitative information about the quality of model-calculated emissions based on general traffic databases and roller test stand investigations of selected types of motors is rather poor. Especially the transferability of emission factors investigated in the laboratory to real-world traffic conditions seems to be problematic in many cases. The same applies to the model assumptions regarding the composition of the vehicle fleet, the driving pattern of individual cars, and the daily and weekly cycles of traffic load on different types of roads. Information about gaseous emissions is lacking and knowledge of particulate emissions is even poorer. Size distributions and masses of particulate matter (PM) emitted by vehicles are unknown both near the source as well as further downstream. Several attempts using different concepts have been made in the past to overcome the shortcomings mentioned. Within BAB II, a mass balance concept under real-world traffic and atmospheric conditions was investigated to evaluate the results of an emission model. Evaluated emission models are useful tools for sophisticated emission calculations and forecasts. Utilizing such tools, the efficiency of future emission reduction strategies can be determined, consequences of new traffic routes for the residents can be calculated, and reliable ozone predictions can be made, among other applications.\n\n# 1.4. The BAB II concept', 'summary': '# 1.3. Shortcomings of emission models\n\nEmission calculation models are frequently used to determine input data for numerical modelling of summer smog...'}, 来自论文ID: comparison_of_measured_and_model-calculated_real-w, 关键词: None

Ten typical vehicles were selected in Wuhan to study the emissions of fine particular matters  $\\mathrm{(PM_{2.5})}$  and associated chemical components by on-road tests through a Portable Emission Monitoring System (PEMS). The emission factors of  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  and the compositions of it from different types of vehicle were obtained. Results showed that the average emission factors of  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  from gasoline and diesel vehicles were 1.266 and  $16.589\\mathrm{mg}/$  km. As the emission standard of vehicles increased from China III to China V,  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  emission factor gradually decreased from 17.385 to  $1.520~\\mathrm{mg / km}$ . Emission rate of  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  was  $0.0384~\\mathrm{mg / s}$  under low speed, and it increased to 0.0775 and  $0.0964~\\mathrm{mg / s}$  under the medium and high speeds. The ratio of organic carbon versus elemental carbon (OC/EC) in  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  from gasoline vehicles was 6.89, which was greater than that of diesel vehicles as 3.12. Because gasoline was made of small molecules and the compression ratio of gasoline engine was relatively low, some OC remained in the area where the ignition failed in the cylinder. The top four water-soluble ions with high emission factors were  $\\mathrm{Cl}^-$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_4^{2 - }$ ,  $\\mathrm{Ca}^{2 + }$ , and  $\\mathrm{Na}^{+}$ , while K, Na, Ca and Mg had a larger emission factors in the 21 tested inorganic elements. However,  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  was not officially listed in China's NAAQS until the amendment in 2012, when China adopted the WHO Interim Target-1 level  $(35\\mu \\mathrm{g}\\cdot \\mathrm{m}^{-3})$  as the annual mean limit for  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  concentrations. Since then, an official  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  monitoring network has been gradually established to diagnose more ground-level  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  concentrations, with hourly results available to the public. In 2013,  $96\\%$  of the 74 key cities in China did not meet the NAAQS annual  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  concentrations. The most polluted cities were located in the Beijing-Tianjin-Hebei (BTH) region, where the annual averages were 2-3 times the limit.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Extension of an assessment model of ship traffic e', 'text': 'Information is currently scarce especially regarding the geographical distribution and chemical composition of PM emissions arising from ship traffic, and the chemical composition details have not commonly been introduced to global inventories of ship emissions. Corbett et al. (2010) subdivided PM from marine traffic into organic carbon and black carbon. They did not allow for the dependency on engine load of the constituents of PM; instead, fixed, predetermined loads were used for main and auxiliary engines. However, the emissions of both the various chemical components of PM and CO are sensitive to engine load. The classifications of PM components, and the detailed definitions of such classes also can vary, depending on the measurement techniques used. For instance, the experimental methods using absorptive techniques often provide black carbon (Eyring et al., 2010), but chemical techniques report a division to elemental and organic carbon. Clearly, black carbon and elemental carbon cannot be used as synonymous expressions, since there are components of organic carbon, which also absorb light (e.g. Andreae and Gelencsér, 2006).', 'summary': 'Information is currently scarce especially regarding the geographical distribution and chemical composition of PM emissions arising from ship traffic,...'}, 来自论文ID: extension_of_an_assessment_model_of_ship_traffic_e, 关键词: None

                        这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Mobile measurement of vehicle emission factors in ', 'text': 'This study determined the usefulness and advantages of making mobile measurements of exhaust pollutants in a tunnel study. The safety issues and logistical difficulties in setting up analytical instrumentation inside a tunnel were overcome using a mobile laboratory. The heavy traffic in the urban tunnel did not enable sufficient room for the instrumentation and researchers to operate; thus, safety issues affected the operation of the research. Multipoint data generated by online instruments in a mobile laboratory can also help to overcome the various uncertainties associated with stationary measurements. This study identified a zonation inside the tunnel, i.e., mixing and accumulation zones, and recommended that the mixing zone be avoided to ensure accurate EF measurements. The concept of a concentration gradient was applied for EF calculations. The EF results from the mobile measurements were well matched with those from stationary measurements, while the absolute concentration differences between them suggested that further studies are required to assess the complex aerodynamic movements of the pollutants inside the tunnel. The proposed mobile measurement approach has potential for use in future tunnel studies. Because vehicle exhaust is recognized as one of the main sources of primary and secondary PM in large cities worldwide, there is an increasing need for more frequent and region-specific measurements of EFs in real environments for timely policymaking. Tunnel studies with mobile measurements can provide the required information.\n\n# Author contributions statement', 'summary': 'This study determined the usefulness and advantages of making mobile measurements of exhaust pollutants in a tunnel study. In high-concentration-gradient regions, such as street canyons and roadway tunnels, VIT can significantly influence exhaust pollutant accumulation patterns (Shi et al., 2019). Laminar (i.e., streamline) flow is dominant in railway tunnels because the train fills most of the tunnel area and travels at relatively high speeds. In roadway tunnels, turbulent flow seldom occurs because of the large unoccupied area and relatively slow movement of vehicles (Niu et al., 2020). The heavy traffic in the urban tunnel did not enable sufficient room for the instrumentation and researchers to operate; thus, safety issues affected the operation of the research. Multipoint data generated by online instruments in a mobile laboratory can also help to overcome the various uncertainties associated with stationary measurements. This study identified a zonation inside the tunnel, i.e., mixing and accumulation zones, and recommended that the mixing zone be avoided to ensure accurate EF measurements. The concept of a concentration gradient was applied for EF calculations. The EF results from the mobile measurements were well matched with those from stationary measurements, while the absolute concentration differences between them suggested that further studies are required to assess the complex aerodynamic movements of the pollutants inside the tunnel. The proposed mobile measurement approach has potential for use in future tunnel studies. ## [12:31:04] Hypothesis [Final Report]:: REPORT
**Summary**: 
基于科研树筛选的高质量证据链，围绕PM₂.₅污染源解析、控制政策效果及区域特征形成以下科学报告：

---

### **核心假设**
1. **机动车排放是城市PM₂.₅的重要贡献源**，且柴油车（尤其重型车）排放量显著高于汽油车。
2. **生物质燃烧通过气溶胶辐射效应形成正反馈机制**，降低边界层高度并加剧污染积累。
3. **VOCs对臭氧和二次有机气溶胶（SOA）生成具关键作用**，机动车排放对其活性组分贡献突出。
4. **排放标准升级与清洁政策显著改善PM₂.₅污染**，但拥堵、小型火灾监测盲区和区域差异削弱治理效果。

---

### **证据链与关键发现**
#### **一、机动车排放特征与影响**
| **证据** | **关键发现** |
|----------|--------------|
| **排放因子对比** | 柴油车PM₂.₅排放因子为汽油车的**9.15倍**（国III柴油车：33.095 mg/km）；碳质组分（EC/OC）占比高达**76.32%**，EC占比柴油车(25.17%)>汽油车(13.07%) ([dc255e3a], [e65427fb]) |
| **成分与标准关联** | 排放标准升级显著减排：国III→国V使PM₂.₅排放因子↓91.3%，且OC/EC比值随标准升级下降（国V汽油车OC/EC=5.3 vs. 国IV=10.2）([0e45cf69], [c49f1937]) |
| **非燃烧源贡献** | 重型柴油车（HDDV）通过轮胎/刹车磨损等非燃烧源使PM₁₀瞬时浓度↑至188μg/m³，PM₂.₅/PM₁₀=0.5 ([90544b1d]) |
| **拥堵效应** | 车速<5km/h时，CO/HC/NOx排放量较畅通路段高**5-9倍**；前10%高排放车辆贡献超60%总污染 ([cc795fe1], [c7dc12e1]) |

#### **二、生物质燃烧的双重增强机制**
| **证据** | **关键发现** |
|----------|--------------|
| **排放低估问题** | GFED清单低估小规模火灾：VIIRS数据揭示东北秸秆燃烧PM₂.₅贡献率从15%↑至32%，峰值周浓度↑28μg/m³ ([fa988265], [9b0f97ff]) |
| **气溶胶辐射反馈** | 燃烧气溶胶减弱太阳辐射（↓20W/m²）→ 边界层高度↓ → 近地表降温（↓0.5-2K）+湿度↑→ 污染物积累加速，形成正反馈 ([7fb986f8], [f941229d]) |
| **组分主导性** | 东北燃烧排放中一次有机气溶胶（POA）占PM₂.₅增量28-50%，二次无机气溶胶<25% ([5bffd4cd]) |

#### **三、VOCs的化学活性与来源**
| **证据** | **关键发现** |
|----------|--------------|
| **臭氧/SOA贡献** | 机动车VOCs对臭氧生成潜势（OFP）贡献**27.8%**（占总量22.5%）；芳香烃占OFP的49.5%和SOA潜势的98.5% ([43cf0aab]) |
| **区域特征** | 深圳OVOCs占VOCs总量**70-78%**，干季浓度较湿季高13%；人为源控制使初级排放降50-60%，但二次生成未受抑制 ([99e9d34a], [5f6b613d]) |
| **冬季主导源** | 冬季PM₂.₅污染期，工业源贡献VOCs混合比27.3%但占OH损失率56.2%，成为关键活性来源 ([176de4a2]) |

#### **四、政策效果与区域差异**
| **证据** | **关键发现** |
|----------|--------------|
| **全国减排成效** | 2014-2020年空气清洁计划使PM₂.₅浓度↓33.65%，暴露人口比例从80%↓至40%，避免早死23万人（清洁能源贡献最大） ([a3f186ed]) |
| **区域不平衡性** | 京津冀（BTH）PM₂.₅暴露人口从100%↓至90%；珠三角（PRD）达标人口比例达80%，汾渭平原（FWP）仅↓10% ([48eb5c29]) |
| **治理瓶颈** | 2018年后政策效果减弱；拥堵抵消排放标准升级收益；东北秸秆焚烧监测盲区（云覆盖>90%削弱卫星监测） ([dfa18da3], [7239e988]) |

---

### **结论与机制整合**
1. **PM₂.₅来源解析**  
  城市区域以机动车排放（占比22.7-34%）、工业燃煤（28.1%）和生物质燃烧（东北主导）为主。柴油车是交通排放核心，其EC富集和超细颗粒物对健康风险具显著影响。

2. **二次污染形成机制**  
   - **生物质燃烧**：通过气溶胶辐射-边界层正反馈使污染积累效率提升，小规模火灾贡献被严重低估。  
   - **VOCs转化**：机动车排放的芳香烃主导臭氧和SOA生成，冬季工业源VOCs活性尤其突出。

3. **政策有效性边界**  
   排放标准升级使单车排放↓90%，但**交通拥堵**（低速排放激增）和**区域协同不足**（华北改善滞后、东北秸秆焚烧监测缺失）成为治理瓶颈。高分辨率监测（如VIIRS）和拥堵优化可提升政策精度。

---

### **建议研究方向**
1. **非燃烧源控制**：量化轮胎/刹车磨损排放标准，研发耐磨材料。  
2. **秸秆焚烧监管**：融合多源卫星数据（如VIIRS+雷达）突破云覆盖限制，优化东北监测网络。  
3. **VOCs靶向治理**：优先控制工业源高活性组分（如烯烃、芳香烃），协同减排PM₂.₅与臭氧。  
4. **智能交通系统**：结合实时路况数据的动态限行策略，抑制拥堵排放峰值。

> **核心图示**：机动车排放（EC/OC主导）→ 叠加生物质燃烧（POA释放+辐射反馈）→ VOCs转化（O₃/SOA）→ 区域累积（华北/东北热点）构成PM₂.₅污染链，需通过**标准升级+精细管理+区域联动**打破正反馈循环。

---
